<!-- ============================================================

     FIREBASE BRIDGE  (type="module")

     ------------------------------------------------------------

     Loads the Firebase SDK from the CDN, connects to Firestore,

     and exposes window.FWC for the main (non-module) script below.


     >>> REPLACE firebaseConfig BELOW with your project's config.

         See FIREBASE-SETUP.md for step-by-step instructions. <<<

     ============================================================ -->

<script type="module">

  import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/12.14.0/firebase-app.js";

  import { getFirestore, doc, getDoc, setDoc, onSnapshot }

    from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/12.14.0/firebase-firestore.js";

  import { getAuth, GoogleAuthProvider, signInWithPopup, signOut, onAuthStateChanged }

    from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/12.14.0/firebase-auth.js";


  // ---- Firebase project config ----

  const firebaseConfig = {

    apiKey: "AIzaSyAxnaayILjQIIGlsot9yry1mslFPOkM0UQ",

    authDomain: "futures-world-cup.firebaseapp.com",

    projectId: "futures-world-cup",

    storageBucket: "futures-world-cup.firebasestorage.app",

    messagingSenderId: "676666367799",

    appId: "1:676666367799:web:352e5347eee5ce0ee544b2",

    measurementId: "G-SJ9N01PWYJ",

  };

  // ---------------------------------


  // ---- ADMIN ALLOWLIST ----------------------------------------------------

  // Only these Google accounts may enter scores. Add/remove emails as needed

  // (lowercase). This is the client-side check; the SAME list must also go in

  // your Firestore security rules — see FIREBASE-SETUP.md.

  const ADMIN_EMAILS = [

    "dfahey@pingry.org",

    "agarcia@pingry.org",

    "rlewis2026@pingry.org",

    "asteinberg@pingry.org",

  ].map(e => e.toLowerCase());


  function isAllowed(email) {

    return !!email && ADMIN_EMAILS.includes(email.toLowerCase());

  }

  // -------------------------------------------------------------------------


  // The single Firestore document that holds the whole tournament's scores.

  const DOC_PATH = ["tournaments", "futures-world-cup"];


  let db = null, auth = null, scoreDocRef = null;

  let firebaseReady = false;


  // Detect whether config has actually been filled in.

  const configured = firebaseConfig.apiKey && firebaseConfig.apiKey !== "REPLACE_ME";


  if (configured) {

    try {

      const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);

      db = getFirestore(app);

      auth = getAuth(app);

      scoreDocRef = doc(db, DOC_PATH[0], DOC_PATH[1]);

      firebaseReady = true;

    } catch (e) {

      console.error("Firebase init failed:", e);

    }

  } else {

    console.warn("Firebase not configured — running in local-only mode. Edit firebaseConfig to enable sync.");

  }


  // Expose a small, stable bridge for the main script.

  // Every method is null-safe so the site still works with no/broken config.

  window.FWC = {

    ready: firebaseReady,


    // Subscribe to live changes. cb receives { scores, assignments, rosters }.

    subscribe(cb) {

      if (!firebaseReady) return;

      onSnapshot(scoreDocRef, (snap) => {

        const data = snap.exists() ? snap.data() : {};

        cb({ scores: data.scores || {}, assignments: data.assignments || {}, rosters: data.rosters || {} });

      }, (err) => console.error("Firestore listen error:", err));

    },


    // Push tournament data to Firestore. Pass any subset of

    // {scores, assignments, rosters}.

    async save(partial) {

      if (!firebaseReady) return Promise.reject(new Error("Firebase not ready"));

      return setDoc(scoreDocRef, { ...partial, updatedAt: Date.now() }, { merge: true });

    },


    // One-time read (used at startup before the listener attaches).

    async fetchOnce() {

      if (!firebaseReady) return null;

      try {

        const snap = await getDoc(scoreDocRef);

        const data = snap.exists() ? snap.data() : {};

        return { scores: data.scores || {}, assignments: data.assignments || {}, rosters: data.rosters || {} };

      } catch (e) { console.error("fetchOnce failed:", e); return null; }

    },


    // Admin sign-in with Google. Resolves with { email, allowed }.

    // If the signed-in account isn't on the allowlist, we sign them back out

    // and report allowed:false so the UI can explain why.

    async login() {

      if (!firebaseReady) return Promise.reject(new Error("Firebase not ready"));

      const provider = new GoogleAuthProvider();

      const cred = await signInWithPopup(auth, provider);

      const email = cred.user.email || "";

      if (!isAllowed(email)) {

        await signOut(auth);

        return { email, allowed: false };

      }

      return { email, allowed: true };

    },


    async logout() {

      if (!firebaseReady) return;

      return signOut(auth);

    },


    // Notify main script when auth state flips. Passes admin status, which is

    // true only when a signed-in user is also on the allowlist.

    onAuthChange(cb) {

      if (!firebaseReady) { cb({ isAdmin: false, email: null }); return; }

      onAuthStateChanged(auth, (user) => {

        const email = user ? (user.email || "") : null;

        cb({ isAdmin: !!user && isAllowed(email), email });

      });

    },

  };


  // Let the main script know the bridge is installed (it may load first).

  window.dispatchEvent(new Event("fwc-firebase-ready"));

</script>


<script>

// ============================================================

// DATA MODEL

// ============================================================


// SLOTS — permanent identifiers used everywhere by the schedule + bracket

// logic. The "label" is the placeholder shown before a team is drawn into the

// slot (e.g. "A1"). Teams are assigned to slots live during the Day 1 draw and

// stored in Firebase (state.assignments), so they sync to every device.

const TEAMS = {

  A1: { label: "A1", group: "A" },

  A2: { label: "A2", group: "A" },

  A3: { label: "A3", group: "A" },

  A4: { label: "A4", group: "A" },

  B1: { label: "B1", group: "B" },

  B2: { label: "B2", group: "B" },

  B3: { label: "B3", group: "B" },

  B4: { label: "B4", group: "B" },

  C1: { label: "C1", group: "C" },

  C2: { label: "C2", group: "C" },

  C3: { label: "C3", group: "C" },

  C4: { label: "C4", group: "C" },

};


// DRAW POOL — the 12 real teams that get drawn into the slots above.

// Each team is a stable entity (id never changes) regardless of which slot it's

// drawn into. `roster` is ready for player names to be added later.

const DRAW_POOL = [

  { id: "arg", name: "Argentina", flag: "🇦🇷", roster: [] },

  { id: "ita", name: "Italy",     flag: "🇮🇹", roster: [] },

  { id: "jpn", name: "Japan",     flag: "🇯🇵", roster: [] },

  { id: "mex", name: "Mexico",    flag: "🇲🇽", roster: [] },

  { id: "bra", name: "Brazil",    flag: "🇧🇷", roster: [] },

  { id: "por", name: "Portugal",  flag: "🇵🇹", roster: [] },

  { id: "fra", name: "France",    flag: "🇫🇷", roster: [] },

  { id: "eng", name: "England",   flag: "🏴󠁧󠁢󠁥󠁮󠁧󠁿", roster: [] },

  { id: "sco", name: "Scotland",  flag: "🏴󠁧󠁢󠁳󠁣󠁴󠁿", roster: [] },

  { id: "esp", name: "Spain",     flag: "🇪🇸", roster: [] },

  { id: "bel", name: "Belgium",   flag: "🇧🇪", roster: [] },

  { id: "cro", name: "Croatia",   flag: "🇭🇷", roster: [] },

];


const POOL_BY_ID = Object.fromEntries(DRAW_POOL.map(t => [t.id, t]));

// ============================================================

// STATE

// ============================================================


let state = {

  scores: {},

  assignments: {},   // slotId -> pool team id  (set during the live draw)

  rosters: {},        // poolTeamId -> [ {num, name, pos}, ... ]

  adminMode: false,   // UI: are edit affordances shown

  isAdmin: false,     // auth: is the user a signed-in, allowlisted admin

  adminEmail: null,   // which account is signed in

  currentDay: 1,

  editingMatchId: null,

};


const STORAGE_KEY = "futures-world-cup-state";


// --- Local cache (always kept in sync as an offline fallback) ---

function loadLocalCache() {

  try {

    const saved = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);

    if (saved) {

      const parsed = JSON.parse(saved);

      state.scores = parsed.scores || {};

      state.assignments = parsed.assignments || {};

      state.rosters = parsed.rosters || {};

    }

  } catch (e) { console.warn("Local load failed:", e); }

}


function writeLocalCache() {

  try {

    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify({

      scores: state.scores,

      assignments: state.assignments,

      rosters: state.rosters,

    }));

  } catch (e) { console.warn("Local save failed:", e); }

}


// Backwards-compatible: existing code calls loadState()/saveState().

function loadState() { loadLocalCache(); }


// Push to Firebase if we're an authenticated admin. `partial` is the subset of

// {scores, assignments, rosters} that changed. Local cache is always updated

// first so the UI stays responsive and works offline.

function pushToCloud(partial) {

  writeLocalCache();

  if (window.FWC && window.FWC.ready && state.isAdmin) {

    setSyncStatus("saving");

    window.FWC.save(partial)

      .then(() => setSyncStatus("synced"))

      .catch(err => {

        console.error("Cloud save failed:", err);

        setSyncStatus("error");

      });

  }

}


// Existing callers save scores.

function saveState() { pushToCloud({ scores: state.scores }); }


// Draw tool saves assignments.

function saveAssignments() { pushToCloud({ assignments: state.assignments }); }


// Roster editor saves rosters.

function saveRosters() { pushToCloud({ rosters: state.rosters }); }


// Visual sync indicator (defined fully later; safe no-op if element missing).

function setSyncStatus(kind) {

  const el = document.getElementById("syncStatus");

  if (!el) return;

  const map = {

    offline: { txt: "Local only", cls: "" },

    connected: { txt: "Live", cls: "live" },

    saving: { txt: "Saving…", cls: "live" },

    synced: { txt: "Live", cls: "live" },

    error: { txt: "Sync error", cls: "err" },

  };

  const s = map[kind] || map.offline;

  el.textContent = s.txt;

  el.className = "sync-status " + s.cls;

}


// ============================================================

// GROUP STANDINGS

// ============================================================


function getGroupStandings(groupLetter) {

  const teams = Object.keys(TEAMS).filter(t => TEAMS[t].group === groupLetter);

  const stats = {};

  teams.forEach(t => {

    stats[t] = { teamId: t, played: 0, won: 0, drawn: 0, lost: 0, gf: 0, ga: 0, pts: 0, h2h: {} };

  });


  DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.filter(m => m.round === "group" && m.group === groupLetter).forEach(m => {

    const score = state.scores[m.id];

    if (!score || score.status !== 'final') return;

    const h = m.home, a = m.away;

    stats[h].played++; stats[a].played++;

    stats[h].gf += score.home; stats[h].ga += score.away;

    stats[a].gf += score.away; stats[a].ga += score.home;

    if (score.home > score.away) {

      stats[h].won++; stats[a].lost++; stats[h].pts += 3;

      stats[h].h2h[a] = 3; stats[a].h2h[h] = 0;

    } else if (score.home < score.away) {

      stats[a].won++; stats[h].lost++; stats[a].pts += 3;

      stats[a].h2h[h] = 3; stats[h].h2h[a] = 0;

    } else {

      stats[h].drawn++; stats[a].drawn++; stats[h].pts += 1; stats[a].pts += 1;

      stats[h].h2h[a] = 1; stats[a].h2h[h] = 1;

    }

  });


  return Object.values(stats).sort((x, y) => {

    if (y.pts !== x.pts) return y.pts - x.pts;

    if (x.h2h[y.teamId] !== undefined && y.h2h[x.teamId] !== undefined) {

      if (y.h2h[x.teamId] !== x.h2h[y.teamId]) return y.h2h[x.teamId] - x.h2h[y.teamId];

    }

    const xGd = x.gf - x.ga, yGd = y.gf - y.ga;

    if (yGd !== xGd) return yGd - xGd;

    return y.gf - x.gf;

  });

}


function getAllGroupsComplete() {

  return ["A","B","C"].every(g => {

    const groupGames = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.filter(m => m.round === "group" && m.group === g);

    return groupGames.every(m => state.scores[m.id]?.status === 'final');

  });

}


function getThirdPlaceTeams() {

  return ["A","B","C"].map(g => {

    const standings = getGroupStandings(g);

    return standings[2] ? { ...standings[2], group: g } : null;

  }).filter(Boolean);

}


function getBestThirdPlace() {

  const thirds = getThirdPlaceTeams();

  return thirds.sort((x, y) => {

    if (y.pts !== x.pts) return y.pts - x.pts;

    const xGd = x.gf - x.ga, yGd = y.gf - y.ga;

    if (yGd !== xGd) return yGd - xGd;

    return y.gf - x.gf;

  });

}


// Teams finishing in a given group position (0=1st,1=2nd,2=3rd,3=4th) across

// all three groups, ranked against each other by the standard tiebreaker.

// Used to seed the Cup quarterfinals (best/2nd-best/3rd-best 1st-place team, etc).

// Returns null until all three groups are complete.

function getRankedByPosition(position) {

  if (!getAllGroupsComplete()) return null;

  const teams = ["A","B","C"].map(g => {

    const s = getGroupStandings(g);

    return s[position] ? { ...s[position], group: g } : null;

  }).filter(Boolean);

  if (teams.length < 3) return null;

  return teams.sort((x, y) => {

    if (y.pts !== x.pts) return y.pts - x.pts;

    const xGd = x.gf - x.ga, yGd = y.gf - y.ga;

    if (yGd !== xGd) return yGd - xGd;

    return y.gf - x.gf;

  });

}


// ============================================================

// BRACKET RESOLUTION

// ============================================================


function getMatchTeam(matchId, side) {

  const match = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.find(m => m.id === matchId);

  if (!match) return null;

  if (side === "home" && match.home) return match.home;

  if (side === "away" && match.away) return match.away;

  if (!match.source) return null;

  return resolveSource(match.source[side]);

}


function resolveSource(src) {

  if (!src) return null;


  const groupResults = (letter) => {

    const groupGames = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.filter(m => m.round === "group" && m.group === letter);

    const complete = groupGames.every(m => state.scores[m.id]?.status === 'final');

    if (!complete) return null;

    return getGroupStandings(letter);

  };


  if (src.startsWith("winner") && src.length === 7) {

    const letter = src[6];

    const s = groupResults(letter);

    return s ? s[0].teamId : null;

  }

  if (src.startsWith("runner") && src.length === 7) {

    const letter = src[6];

    const s = groupResults(letter);

    return s ? s[1].teamId : null;

  }

  if (src.startsWith("fourth") && src.length === 7) {

    const letter = src[6];

    const s = groupResults(letter);

    return s ? s[3].teamId : null;

  }

  // Ranked seeding tokens: best1st1..3, best2nd1..3, best3rd1..3

  // (Nth best team finishing in that group position, across all groups.)

  const ranked = src.match(/^best(1st|2nd|3rd)([123])$/);

  if (ranked) {

    const pos = { "1st": 0, "2nd": 1, "3rd": 2 }[ranked[1]];

    const rank = parseInt(ranked[2], 10) - 1; // 1->0, 2->1, 3->2

    const list = getRankedByPosition(pos);

    return list ? list[rank].teamId : null;

  }

  // Back-compat alias: worst3rd === best3rd3

  if (src === "worst3rd") {

    const list = getRankedByPosition(2);

    return list ? list[2].teamId : null;

  }


  const m = src.match(/^(winner|loser)(.+)$/);

  if (m) {

    const role = m[1];

    const refMatchId = m[2];

    const sourceMatch = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.find(mm => mm.id === refMatchId);

    if (!sourceMatch) return null;

    const score = state.scores[refMatchId];

    if (!score || score.status !== 'final') return null;

    const homeTeam = getMatchTeam(refMatchId, "home");

    const awayTeam = getMatchTeam(refMatchId, "away");

    if (!homeTeam || !awayTeam) return null;

    if (score.home === score.away) return null;

    const winner = score.home > score.away ? homeTeam : awayTeam;

    const loser = score.home > score.away ? awayTeam : homeTeam;

    return role === "winner" ? winner : loser;

  }


  return null;

}


// Resolve a slot (A1, B3, …) to its assigned pool team, or null if undrawn.

function getAssignedTeam(slotId) {

  const poolId = state.assignments[slotId];

  return poolId ? POOL_BY_ID[poolId] : null;

}


function getTeamDisplayName(slotId) {

  if (!slotId) return "TBD";

  const t = getAssignedTeam(slotId);

  if (t) return t.name;

  // Not yet drawn: show the placeholder label (e.g. "A1").

  return TEAMS[slotId]?.label || slotId;

}


function getTeamFlag(slotId) {

  if (!slotId) return "";

  const t = getAssignedTeam(slotId);

  return t ? (t.flag || "") : "";

}


// True if this slot still shows a placeholder (used to style undrawn teams).

function isSlotUndrawn(slotId) {

  return !!TEAMS[slotId] && !state.assignments[slotId];

}


// ============================================================

// RENDERING

// ============================================================


function renderGroupStandings(container) {

  container.innerHTML = "";

  ["A","B","C"].forEach(letter => {

    const standings = getGroupStandings(letter);

    const card = document.createElement("div");

    card.className = "group-card";


    const allComplete = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.filter(m => m.round === "group" && m.group === letter)

      .every(m => state.scores[m.id]?.status === 'final');

    const anyPlayed = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.filter(m => m.round === "group" && m.group === letter)

      .some(m => state.scores[m.id]?.status === 'final');


    let tag = "Not started";

    if (allComplete) tag = "Complete";

    else if (anyPlayed) tag = "In progress";


    card.innerHTML = `

      <div class="group-header">

        <div class="group-name">Group ${letter}</div>

        <div class="group-tag">${tag}</div>

      </div>

      <table class="standings-table">

        <thead>

          <tr>

            <th>Team</th>

            <th>P</th><th>W</th><th>D</th><th>L</th>

            <th>GF</th><th>GA</th><th>GD</th><th>PTS</th>

          </tr>

        </thead>

        <tbody>

          ${standings.map((s, i) => `

            <tr class="pos-${i+1}">

              <td class="team-cell"><span class="pos-marker">${i+1}</span><span class="flag">${getTeamFlag(s.teamId)}</span>${getTeamDisplayName(s.teamId)}</td>

              <td>${s.played}</td>

              <td>${s.won}</td>

              <td>${s.drawn}</td>

              <td>${s.lost}</td>

              <td>${s.gf}</td>

              <td>${s.ga}</td>

              <td>${s.gf - s.ga > 0 ? '+' : ''}${s.gf - s.ga}</td>

              <td class="pts">${s.pts}</td>

            </tr>

          `).join("")}

        </tbody>

      </table>

    `;

    container.appendChild(card);

  });

}


function getMatchRoundLabel(match) {

  switch (match.round) {

    case "group": return `Group ${match.group}`;

    case "cup-qf": return `Cup · ${match.label}`;

    case "cup-sf": return `Cup · ${match.label}`;

    case "cup-3rd": return `Cup · 3rd Place`;

    case "cup-final": return `Cup Final`;

    case "shield-qf": return `Shield · ${match.label}`;

    case "shield-sf": return `Shield · ${match.label}`;

    case "shield-final": return `Shield Final`;

    case "friendly": return `${match.label}`;

    default: return match.label || match.round;

  }

}


function formatTime(t) {

  const [h, m] = t.split(":").map(Number);

  const period = h >= 12 ? "PM" : "AM";

  const hour = h > 12 ? h - 12 : (h === 0 ? 12 : h);

  return { time: `${hour}:${m.toString().padStart(2,'0')}`, period };

}


function renderMatchRow(match) {

  const homeId = getMatchTeam(match.id, "home");

  const awayId = getMatchTeam(match.id, "away");

  const score = state.scores[match.id];

  const homeName = getTeamDisplayName(homeId);

  const awayName = getTeamDisplayName(awayId);

  const homeFlag = getTeamFlag(homeId);

  const awayFlag = getTeamFlag(awayId);


  let statusClass = "status-scheduled";

  let statusText = "Scheduled";

  let rowClass = "";

  if (score?.status === 'live') { statusClass = "status-live"; statusText = "Live"; rowClass = "live"; }

  else if (score?.status === 'final') { statusClass = "status-final"; statusText = "Final"; rowClass = "final"; }


  const tf = formatTime(match.time);


  let homeTeamClass = "match-team home";

  let awayTeamClass = "match-team away";

  if (!homeId) homeTeamClass += " tbd";

  if (!awayId) awayTeamClass += " tbd";

  if (score?.status === 'final' && homeId && awayId) {

    if (score.home > score.away) { awayTeamClass += " loser"; }

    else if (score.home < score.away) { homeTeamClass += " loser"; }

  }


  const div = document.createElement("div");

  div.className = `match-row ${rowClass}`;

  div.dataset.matchId = match.id;


  div.innerHTML = `

    <div>

      <div class="match-time">${tf.time}<span class="ampm">${tf.period}</span></div>

      <div class="match-round">${getMatchRoundLabel(match)}</div>

    </div>

    <div class="match-field">${match.field}</div>

    <div class="${homeTeamClass}">

      <span class="name">${homeName}</span>

      <span class="flag">${homeFlag}</span>

    </div>

    <div class="match-score ${!score ? 'empty' : ''}">

      ${score ? `${score.home}<span class="dash">–</span>${score.away}` : 'VS'}

    </div>

    <div class="${awayTeamClass}">

      <span class="flag">${awayFlag}</span>

      <span class="name">${awayName}</span>

    </div>

    <div class="match-status ${statusClass}">${statusText}</div>

  `;


  const resolved = homeId && awayId;

  const isFinal = score?.status === 'final';

  if (resolved && (state.adminMode || isFinal)) {

    div.classList.add("admin-mode");

    div.addEventListener("click", () => {

      if (state.adminMode) openScoreModal(match.id);

      else openResultsModal(match.id);

    });

  }


  return div;

}


function renderScheduleDay(day) {

  const container = document.createElement("div");

  container.className = "schedule-grid";

  const dayMatches = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.filter(m => m.day === day).sort((a, b) => {

    if (a.time !== b.time) return a.time.localeCompare(b.time);

    return a.field.localeCompare(b.field);

  });


  if (dayMatches.length === 0) {

    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state">No matches scheduled.</div>';

    return container;

  }


  const slots = {};

  dayMatches.forEach(m => {

    if (!slots[m.time]) slots[m.time] = [];

    slots[m.time].push(m);

  });


  Object.keys(slots).sort().forEach(time => {

    const tf = formatTime(time);

    const slotHeader = document.createElement("div");

    slotHeader.className = "time-block-label";

    slotHeader.textContent = `${tf.time} ${tf.period}`;

    container.appendChild(slotHeader);

    slots[time].forEach(m => container.appendChild(renderMatchRow(m)));

  });


  return container;

}


function renderSchedule() {

  const tabs = document.getElementById("day-tabs");

  const days = document.getElementById("schedule-days");

  tabs.innerHTML = "";

  days.innerHTML = "";


  DAYS.forEach(d => {

    const tab = document.createElement("button");

    tab.className = "day-tab" + (d.num === state.currentDay ? " active" : "");

    tab.innerHTML = `<span class="day-num">Day ${d.num}</span>${d.label}`;

    tab.addEventListener("click", () => {

      state.currentDay = d.num;

      renderSchedule();

    });

    tabs.appendChild(tab);


    const content = document.createElement("div");

    content.className = "day-content" + (d.num === state.currentDay ? " active" : "");

    content.appendChild(renderScheduleDay(d.num));

    days.appendChild(content);

  });

}


function renderBracketMatch(match, special) {

  const homeId = getMatchTeam(match.id, "home");

  const awayId = getMatchTeam(match.id, "away");

  const score = state.scores[match.id];


  let homeClass = "bracket-team", awayClass = "bracket-team";

  if (!homeId) homeClass += " tbd";

  if (!awayId) awayClass += " tbd";


  if (score?.status === 'final' && homeId && awayId) {

    if (score.home > score.away) { homeClass += " winner"; awayClass += " loser"; }

    else if (score.home < score.away) { awayClass += " winner"; homeClass += " loser"; }

  }


  let matchClass = "bracket-match";

  if (special) matchClass += ` ${special}`;

  if (score?.status === 'final') matchClass += " completed";

  if (score?.status === 'live') matchClass += " live";


  const tf = formatTime(match.time);

  const div = document.createElement("div");

  div.className = matchClass;

  div.dataset.matchId = match.id;


  div.innerHTML = `

    <div class="bracket-match-header">

      <span>${match.label || match.id}</span>

      <span>D${match.day} · ${tf.time}${tf.period}</span>

    </div>

    <div class="${homeClass}">

      <div class="bracket-team-name">

        <span class="flag">${getTeamFlag(homeId)}</span>

        <span class="name">${getTeamDisplayName(homeId)}</span>

      </div>

      <span class="bracket-team-score">${score ? score.home : '—'}</span>

    </div>

    <div class="${awayClass}">

      <div class="bracket-team-name">

        <span class="flag">${getTeamFlag(awayId)}</span>

        <span class="name">${getTeamDisplayName(awayId)}</span>

      </div>

      <span class="bracket-team-score">${score ? score.away : '—'}</span>

    </div>

  `;


  const resolved = homeId && awayId;

  const isFinal = score?.status === 'final';

  if (resolved && (state.adminMode || isFinal)) {

    div.classList.add("admin-mode");

    div.addEventListener("click", () => {

      if (state.adminMode) openScoreModal(match.id);

      else openResultsModal(match.id);

    });

  }


  return div;

}


function renderCupBracket() {

  const container = document.getElementById("cup-bracket");

  container.innerHTML = "";


  const cols = [

    { header: "Quarterfinals", matches: ["CQF1","CQF2","CQF3","CQF4"] },

    { header: "Semifinals", matches: ["CSF1","CSF2"] },

    { header: "3rd Place", matches: ["C3P"] },

    { header: "Final", matches: ["CF"], special: "cup-final" },

  ];


  cols.forEach(col => {

    const colDiv = document.createElement("div");

    colDiv.className = "bracket-col";

    const header = document.createElement("div");

    header.className = "bracket-col-header";

    header.textContent = col.header;

    colDiv.appendChild(header);

    col.matches.forEach(mid => {

      const match = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.find(m => m.id === mid);

      if (match) colDiv.appendChild(renderBracketMatch(match, col.special));

    });

    container.appendChild(colDiv);

  });

}


function renderShieldBracket() {

  const container = document.getElementById("shield-bracket");

  container.innerHTML = "";


  const cols = [

    { header: "Quarterfinals", matches: ["SQF1","SQF2","SQF3","SQF4"] },

    { header: "Semifinals", matches: ["SSF1","SSF2"] },

    { header: "Friendlies", matches: ["FR1","FR2"] },

    { header: "Final", matches: ["SF"] },

  ];


  cols.forEach(col => {

    const colDiv = document.createElement("div");

    colDiv.className = "bracket-col";

    const header = document.createElement("div");

    header.className = "bracket-col-header";

    header.textContent = col.header;

    colDiv.appendChild(header);

    col.matches.forEach(mid => {

      const match = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.find(m => m.id === mid);

      if (match) colDiv.appendChild(renderBracketMatch(match));

    });

    container.appendChild(colDiv);

  });

}


function renderOverviewToday() {

  const container = document.getElementById("overview-today");

  container.innerHTML = "";


  let activeDay = 1;

  for (let d = 1; d <= 4; d++) {

    const dayMatches = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.filter(m => m.day === d);

    const allDone = dayMatches.every(m => state.scores[m.id]?.status === 'final');

    if (!allDone) { activeDay = d; break; }

  }


  const dayLabel = document.createElement("div");

  dayLabel.style.cssText = "font-family: 'Fraunces', serif; font-size: 19px; color: var(--text-soft); margin-bottom: 20px; font-style: italic;";

  dayLabel.textContent = `Day ${activeDay} · ${DAYS[activeDay-1].label}`;

  container.appendChild(dayLabel);


  container.appendChild(renderScheduleDay(activeDay));


  const liveMatches = Object.entries(state.scores).filter(([_, s]) => s.status === 'live');

  const finalsCount = Object.values(state.scores).filter(s => s.status === 'final').length;

  const totalMatches = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.length;

  const liveEl = document.getElementById("live-indicator");

  if (liveMatches.length > 0) {

    liveEl.innerHTML = `<span class="live-dot"></span><span style="color: var(--orange); font-weight: 700;">${liveMatches.length} match${liveMatches.length > 1 ? 'es' : ''} live now</span>`;

  } else if (finalsCount === 0) {

    liveEl.textContent = "Tournament not yet started";

  } else if (finalsCount === totalMatches) {

    liveEl.innerHTML = `<span style="color: var(--green); font-weight: 700;">Tournament complete</span>`;

  } else {

    liveEl.textContent = `${finalsCount} of ${totalMatches} matches complete`;

  }

}


function render() {

  renderGroupStandings(document.getElementById("overview-groups"));

  renderGroupStandings(document.getElementById("groups-full"));

  renderTeams();

  renderLeaders();

  renderSchedule();

  renderCupBracket();

  renderShieldBracket();

  renderOverviewToday();

  renderDraw();

}


// ============================================================

// TEAMS

// ============================================================


// Which group/slot a pool team has been drawn into (label like "A2"), or null.

function groupLabelForPoolId(poolId) {

  const slot = SLOT_ORDER.find(s => state.assignments[s] === poolId);

  return slot ? { group: TEAMS[slot].group, label: TEAMS[slot].label } : null;

}


// Escape user-entered text before putting it in HTML.

function esc(s) {

  return String(s == null ? "" : s)

    .replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;")

    .replace(/"/g, "&quot;").replace(/'/g, "&#39;");

}


const ROSTER_MAX = 10; // up to 10 players per team


// The live roster for a team: synced data if present, else the pool default.

function getRoster(poolId) {

  if (Array.isArray(state.rosters[poolId])) return state.rosters[poolId];

  const t = POOL_BY_ID[poolId];

  return (t && Array.isArray(t.roster)) ? t.roster : [];

}


function renderTeams() {

  const grid = document.getElementById("teams-grid");

  if (!grid) return;


  grid.innerHTML = DRAW_POOL.map(team => {

    const placed = groupLabelForPoolId(team.id);

    const groupLine = placed

      ? `<div class="tc-group">Group ${placed.group} · ${placed.label}</div>`

      : `<div class="tc-group undrawn">Not yet drawn</div>`;

    const flag = team.flag ? `<span class="tc-flag">${team.flag}</span>` : "";


    // Build a fixed 10-row table with a header. Rows with a player show their

    // data; the rest stay as blank numbered placeholders until the CSV loads.

    const roster = getRoster(team.id);

    const namedCount = roster.filter(p => p && (p.name || "").trim()).length;


    const rowsHtml = [];

    for (let i = 0; i < ROSTER_MAX; i++) {

      const p = roster[i] || {};

      const hasName = (p.name || "").trim();

      rowsHtml.push(`

        <tr class="${hasName ? "" : "blank-row"}">

          <td class="r-rownum">${i + 1}</td>

          <td class="r-jersey">${p.jersey != null && p.jersey !== "" ? esc(p.jersey) : ""}</td>

          <td class="r-name">${hasName ? esc(p.name) : ""}</td>

          <td class="r-pos">${esc(p.pos || "")}</td>

          <td class="r-grade">${esc(p.grade || "")}</td>

        </tr>`);

    }

    const rosterBody = `

      <table class="roster-table">

        <thead>

          <tr>

            <th class="r-rownum">#</th>

            <th class="r-jersey">No.</th>

            <th class="r-name">Name</th>

            <th class="r-pos">Pos</th>

            <th class="r-grade">Gr</th>

          </tr>

        </thead>

        <tbody>${rowsHtml.join("")}</tbody>

      </table>`;


    const sizeLabel = `${namedCount} player${namedCount === 1 ? "" : "s"}`;


    const editBtn = state.adminMode

      ? `<button class="roster-edit-btn" data-team="${team.id}">Edit roster</button>`

      : "";


    return `

      <div class="team-card">

        <div class="team-card-top">

          ${flag}

          <div>

            <div class="tc-name">${esc(team.name)}</div>

            ${groupLine}

          </div>

        </div>

        <div class="tc-roster">

          <div class="tc-roster-label">Roster <span class="tc-roster-count">${sizeLabel}</span></div>

          ${rosterBody}

          ${editBtn}

        </div>

      </div>`;

  }).join("");


  if (state.adminMode) {

    grid.querySelectorAll(".roster-edit-btn").forEach(btn => {

      btn.addEventListener("click", () => openRosterModal(btn.dataset.team));

    });

  }

}


// ============================================================

// LEADERS (tournament-wide stat rollup)

// ============================================================


function aggregateStat(stat) {

  const tally = {};

  Object.keys(state.scores).forEach(matchId => {

    const sc = state.scores[matchId];

    if (!sc || !sc.events || !sc.events[stat]) return;

    const homeName = getTeamDisplayName(getMatchTeam(matchId, "home"));

    const awayName = getTeamDisplayName(getMatchTeam(matchId, "away"));

    sc.events[stat].forEach(e => {

      const teamName = e.team === "away" ? awayName : homeName;

      const key = `${e.player}||${teamName}`;

      if (!tally[key]) tally[key] = { player: e.player, team: teamName, count: 0 };

      tally[key].count++;

    });

  });

  return Object.values(tally).sort((a, b) =>

    b.count - a.count || a.player.localeCompare(b.player)

  );

}


function renderLeaders() {

  const grid = document.getElementById("leaders-grid");

  if (!grid) return;

  const boards = [

    { key: "goals",   title: "Top Scorers", unit: "G" },

    { key: "assists", title: "Top Assists", unit: "A" },

    { key: "saves",   title: "Most Saves",  unit: "S" },

  ];

  grid.innerHTML = boards.map(b => {

    const rows = aggregateStat(b.key).slice(0, 10);

    const body = rows.length

      ? rows.map((r, i) => `

          <div class="lb-row">

            <span class="lb-rank">${i + 1}</span>

            <span class="lb-player">${esc(r.player)}</span>

            <span class="lb-team">${esc(r.team)}</span>

            <span class="lb-count">${r.count}<span class="lb-unit">${b.unit}</span></span>

          </div>`).join("")

      : `<div class="lb-empty">No ${b.key} recorded yet.</div>`;

    return `

      <div class="leaderboard">

        <div class="lb-head">${b.title}</div>

        <div class="lb-rows">${body}</div>

      </div>`;

  }).join("");

}


// ============================================================

// ROSTER EDITOR (admin)

// ============================================================


let rosterEditingTeam = null; // poolId being edited, or null


function openRosterModal(poolId) {

  if (!state.adminMode) return;

  rosterEditingTeam = poolId;

  const team = POOL_BY_ID[poolId];

  document.getElementById("roster-modal-eyebrow").textContent = "Edit Roster";

  document.getElementById("roster-modal-title").innerHTML =

    `${team.flag ? team.flag + " " : ""}${esc(team.name)}`;

  document.getElementById("roster-modal-sub").textContent =

    `Up to ${ROSTER_MAX} players. Leave a row blank to skip it.`;


  const existing = getRoster(poolId);

  const rows = [];

  for (let i = 0; i < ROSTER_MAX; i++) {

    const p = existing[i] || {};

    rows.push(`

      <div class="roster-row">

        <span class="r-rowidx">${i + 1}</span>

        <input class="r-in r-in-jersey" type="text" inputmode="numeric" maxlength="3"

               value="${esc(p.jersey != null ? p.jersey : "")}" placeholder="No." data-i="${i}" data-f="jersey">

        <input class="r-in r-in-name" type="text" maxlength="40"

               value="${esc(p.name || "")}" placeholder="Player name" data-i="${i}" data-f="name">

        <input class="r-in r-in-pos" type="text" maxlength="16"

               value="${esc(p.pos || "")}" placeholder="Position" data-i="${i}" data-f="pos">

        <input class="r-in r-in-grade" type="text" maxlength="6"

               value="${esc(p.grade || "")}" placeholder="Grade" data-i="${i}" data-f="grade">

      </div>`);

  }

  document.getElementById("roster-rows").innerHTML = rows.join("");

  document.getElementById("roster-modal").classList.add("active");

}


function closeRosterModal() {

  document.getElementById("roster-modal").classList.remove("active");

  rosterEditingTeam = null;

}


function saveRosterEdits() {

  if (!state.isAdmin || !rosterEditingTeam) { closeRosterModal(); return; }

  const inputs = document.querySelectorAll("#roster-rows .r-in");

  const draft = [];

  for (let i = 0; i < ROSTER_MAX; i++) draft[i] = { jersey: "", name: "", pos: "", grade: "" };

  inputs.forEach(inp => {

    const i = parseInt(inp.dataset.i, 10);

    draft[i][inp.dataset.f] = inp.value.trim();

  });

  // Keep only rows that have a name; drop fully-empty rows.

  const cleaned = draft.filter(p => p.name);

  state.rosters[rosterEditingTeam] = cleaned;

  saveRosters();

  closeRosterModal();

  render();

}


// ============================================================

// DRAW TOOL

// ============================================================


const SLOT_ORDER = Object.keys(TEAMS); // A1..C4 in definition order


// Slots that still have no team assigned, in order.

function openSlots() {

  return SLOT_ORDER.filter(s => !state.assignments[s]);

}


// Pool team ids not yet assigned to any slot.

function undrawnPoolIds() {

  const used = new Set(Object.values(state.assignments));

  return DRAW_POOL.map(t => t.id).filter(id => !used.has(id));

}


// Which slot a given pool team is currently in (or null).

function slotForPoolId(poolId) {

  return SLOT_ORDER.find(s => state.assignments[s] === poolId) || null;

}


let lastDrawnSlot = null; // for the flash highlight


function renderDraw() {

  const grid = document.getElementById("draw-grid");

  if (!grid) return;


  const groups = ["A", "B", "C"];

  grid.innerHTML = groups.map(g => {

    const slots = SLOT_ORDER.filter(s => TEAMS[s].group === g);

    return `

      <div class="draw-group">

        <div class="draw-group-head">Group ${g}</div>

        ${slots.map(s => {

          const team = getAssignedTeam(s);

          const empty = team ? "" : "empty";

          const adminCls = state.adminMode ? "admin" : "";

          const flash = (s === lastDrawnSlot) ? "just-drawn" : "";

          const flag = team && team.flag ? `<span class="slot-flag">${team.flag}</span>` : "";

          const nameTxt = team ? team.name : "— empty —";

          return `<div class="draw-slot ${empty} ${adminCls} ${flash}" data-slot="${s}">

            <span class="slot-tag">${TEAMS[s].label}</span>

            ${flag}

            <span class="slot-name">${nameTxt}</span>

          </div>`;

        }).join("")}

      </div>`;

  }).join("");


  // Bind clicks for admin direct-assign.

  if (state.adminMode) {

    grid.querySelectorAll(".draw-slot").forEach(el => {

      el.addEventListener("click", () => openDrawModal(el.dataset.slot));

    });

  }


  const remaining = undrawnPoolIds().length;

  const remEl = document.getElementById("draw-remaining");

  if (remEl) {

    remEl.textContent = remaining === 0

      ? "All teams drawn."

      : `${remaining} team${remaining === 1 ? "" : "s"} left · ${openSlots().length} open slot${openSlots().length === 1 ? "" : "s"}`;

  }

  const randBtn = document.getElementById("draw-random");

  if (randBtn) randBtn.disabled = (remaining === 0 || openSlots().length === 0);


  lastDrawnSlot = null; // flash only once

}


// Pull a random undrawn team into the next open slot.

function drawRandom() {

  if (!state.isAdmin) return;

  const pool = undrawnPoolIds();

  const slots = openSlots();

  if (pool.length === 0 || slots.length === 0) return;

  const poolId = pool[Math.floor(Math.random() * pool.length)];

  const slot = slots[0];

  state.assignments[slot] = poolId;

  lastDrawnSlot = slot;

  saveAssignments();

  render();

}


// Direct-assign modal: pick which team goes in this slot (or reassign/clear).

let drawEditingSlot = null;


function openDrawModal(slotId) {

  if (!state.adminMode) return;

  drawEditingSlot = slotId;

  document.getElementById("draw-modal-title").textContent = `Slot ${TEAMS[slotId].label}`;

  const current = getAssignedTeam(slotId);

  document.getElementById("draw-modal-sub").textContent = current

    ? `Currently: ${current.name}. Pick a different team or clear.`

    : "Pick the team that was drawn into this slot.";


  const list = document.getElementById("draw-pick-list");

  list.innerHTML = DRAW_POOL.map(t => {

    const where = slotForPoolId(t.id);

    const takenElsewhere = where && where !== slotId;

    const isHere = where === slotId;

    const flag = t.flag ? `<span>${t.flag}</span>` : "";

    const tag = isHere

      ? `<span class="pick-where">here</span>`

      : (takenElsewhere ? `<span class="pick-where">${TEAMS[where].label}</span>` : "");

    return `<button class="draw-pick ${takenElsewhere ? "taken" : ""}" data-pool="${t.id}" ${takenElsewhere ? "disabled" : ""}>

      ${flag}<span>${t.name}</span>${tag}

    </button>`;

  }).join("");


  list.querySelectorAll(".draw-pick:not(.taken)").forEach(btn => {

    btn.addEventListener("click", () => assignSlot(slotId, btn.dataset.pool));

  });


  document.getElementById("draw-modal-clear").style.display = current ? "inline-flex" : "none";

  document.getElementById("draw-modal").classList.add("active");

}


function closeDrawModal() {

  document.getElementById("draw-modal").classList.remove("active");

  drawEditingSlot = null;

}


function assignSlot(slotId, poolId) {

  if (!state.isAdmin) return;

  state.assignments[slotId] = poolId;

  lastDrawnSlot = slotId;

  saveAssignments();

  closeDrawModal();

  render();

}


function clearDrawSlot() {

  if (!state.isAdmin || !drawEditingSlot) return;

  delete state.assignments[drawEditingSlot];

  saveAssignments();

  closeDrawModal();

  render();

}


function resetDraw() {

  if (!state.isAdmin) return;

  if (!confirm("Clear ALL draw assignments? Every slot goes back to its placeholder.")) return;

  state.assignments = {};

  saveAssignments();

  render();

}


// ============================================================

// MODAL

// ============================================================


// Working buffer for the match's events while the editor is open.

let editEvents = { goals: [], assists: [], saves: [] };


function openScoreModal(matchId) {

  const match = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.find(m => m.id === matchId);

  if (!match) return;

  const homeId = getMatchTeam(matchId, "home");

  const awayId = getMatchTeam(matchId, "away");

  if (!homeId || !awayId) return;


  state.editingMatchId = matchId;

  document.getElementById("modal-eyebrow").textContent = getMatchRoundLabel(match);

  document.getElementById("modal-title").textContent = "Final Score";

  document.getElementById("modal-sub").textContent = `${match.field} · Day ${match.day}, ${formatTime(match.time).time} ${formatTime(match.time).period}`;

  document.getElementById("modal-home").innerHTML = `${getTeamFlag(homeId)} ${getTeamDisplayName(homeId)}`;

  document.getElementById("modal-away").innerHTML = `${getTeamDisplayName(awayId)} ${getTeamFlag(awayId)}`;


  const existing = state.scores[matchId];

  document.getElementById("modal-home-score").value = existing ? existing.home : "";

  document.getElementById("modal-away-score").value = existing ? existing.away : "";


  // Load existing events into the working buffer (deep copy).

  const ev = (existing && existing.events) || {};

  editEvents = {

    goals:   (ev.goals   || []).map(e => ({ ...e })),

    assists: (ev.assists || []).map(e => ({ ...e })),

    saves:   (ev.saves   || []).map(e => ({ ...e })),

  };

  renderStatRows();


  document.getElementById("modal").classList.add("active");

  setTimeout(() => document.getElementById("modal-home-score").focus(), 50);

}


// Build the player <option> list for a given slot (resolved team), from roster.

function playerOptionsFor(teamSlotId, selectedName) {

  const poolId = state.assignments[teamSlotId];

  const roster = poolId ? getRoster(poolId).filter(p => (p.name || "").trim()) : [];

  let opts = `<option value="">— player —</option>`;

  roster.forEach(p => {

    const label = p.jersey ? `#${p.jersey} ${p.name}` : p.name;

    const sel = (p.name === selectedName) ? " selected" : "";

    opts += `<option value="${esc(p.name)}"${sel}>${esc(label)}</option>`;

  });

  // Free-text fallback option.

  const customSel = (selectedName && !roster.some(p => p.name === selectedName)) ? " selected" : "";

  opts += `<option value="__custom__"${customSel}>Other (type name)…</option>`;

  return opts;

}


function renderStatRows() {

  const matchId = state.editingMatchId;

  const homeId = getMatchTeam(matchId, "home");

  const awayId = getMatchTeam(matchId, "away");

  const homeName = getTeamDisplayName(homeId);

  const awayName = getTeamDisplayName(awayId);


  ["goals", "assists", "saves"].forEach(stat => {

    const container = document.getElementById("rows-" + stat);

    container.innerHTML = editEvents[stat].map((e, i) => {

      const teamSlot = (e.team === "away") ? awayId : homeId;

      const poolId = state.assignments[teamSlot];

      const roster = poolId ? getRoster(poolId).filter(p => (p.name || "").trim()) : [];

      const isCustom = e.player && !roster.some(p => p.name === e.player);

      return `

        <div class="stat-row" data-stat="${stat}" data-i="${i}">

          <select class="stat-team" data-f="team">

            <option value="home"${e.team !== "away" ? " selected" : ""}>${esc(homeName)}</option>

            <option value="away"${e.team === "away" ? " selected" : ""}>${esc(awayName)}</option>

          </select>

          <select class="stat-player" data-f="player">

            ${playerOptionsFor(teamSlot, e.player)}

          </select>

          <input class="stat-custom" data-f="custom" type="text" maxlength="40" placeholder="Player name"

                 value="${isCustom ? esc(e.player) : ""}" style="${isCustom ? "" : "display:none;"}">

          <button class="stat-remove" data-remove="${stat}:${i}" title="Remove">×</button>

        </div>`;

    }).join("");

  });


  // Bind row interactions.

  document.querySelectorAll("#stats-editor .stat-row").forEach(row => {

    const stat = row.dataset.stat, i = parseInt(row.dataset.i, 10);

    row.querySelector(".stat-team").addEventListener("change", e => {

      editEvents[stat][i].team = e.target.value;

      editEvents[stat][i].player = ""; // reset player when team changes

      renderStatRows();

    });

    const playerSel = row.querySelector(".stat-player");

    const customInp = row.querySelector(".stat-custom");

    playerSel.addEventListener("change", e => {

      if (e.target.value === "__custom__") {

        customInp.style.display = "";

        editEvents[stat][i].player = customInp.value.trim();

        customInp.focus();

      } else {

        customInp.style.display = "none";

        editEvents[stat][i].player = e.target.value;

      }

    });

    customInp.addEventListener("input", e => {

      editEvents[stat][i].player = e.target.value.trim();

    });

  });

  document.querySelectorAll("#stats-editor .stat-remove").forEach(btn => {

    btn.addEventListener("click", () => {

      const [stat, idx] = btn.dataset.remove.split(":");

      editEvents[stat].splice(parseInt(idx, 10), 1);

      renderStatRows();

      updateStatsNote();

    });

  });

  document.querySelectorAll("#stats-editor .stat-add").forEach(btn => {

    btn.onclick = () => {

      const stat = btn.dataset.add;

      editEvents[stat].push({ team: "home", player: "" });

      renderStatRows();

      updateStatsNote();

    };

  });

  updateStatsNote();

}


// Gentle reconciliation hint: compare goal count to score (doesn't block saving).

function updateStatsNote() {

  const note = document.getElementById("stats-note");

  const h = parseInt(document.getElementById("modal-home-score").value);

  const a = parseInt(document.getElementById("modal-away-score").value);

  if (isNaN(h) || isNaN(a)) { note.textContent = ""; return; }

  const goalsHome = editEvents.goals.filter(e => e.team !== "away").length;

  const goalsAway = editEvents.goals.filter(e => e.team === "away").length;

  const msgs = [];

  if (goalsHome !== h) msgs.push(`home goals logged: ${goalsHome} of ${h}`);

  if (goalsAway !== a) msgs.push(`away goals logged: ${goalsAway} of ${a}`);

  note.textContent = msgs.length ? `Heads up — ${msgs.join(", ")}. (You can still save; scorers are optional.)` : "";

}


function closeModal() {

  document.getElementById("modal").classList.remove("active");

  state.editingMatchId = null;

}


function saveScore() {

  if (!state.isAdmin) { closeModal(); return; }

  const home = parseInt(document.getElementById("modal-home-score").value);

  const away = parseInt(document.getElementById("modal-away-score").value);

  if (isNaN(home) || isNaN(away) || home < 0 || away < 0) {

    alert("Please enter valid scores (0 or higher) for both teams.");

    return;

  }


  const match = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.find(m => m.id === state.editingMatchId);

  if (home === away && match && !["group", "friendly"].includes(match.round)) {

    if (!confirm("Knockout matches typically can't end in a tie. Save anyway? You'll resolve the winner separately.")) {

      return;

    }

  }


  // Clean events: keep only rows with a player name.

  const clean = {};

  ["goals", "assists", "saves"].forEach(stat => {

    clean[stat] = editEvents[stat]

      .filter(e => (e.player || "").trim())

      .map(e => ({ team: e.team === "away" ? "away" : "home", player: e.player.trim() }));

  });


  state.scores[state.editingMatchId] = { home, away, status: 'final', events: clean };

  saveState();

  closeModal();

  render();

}


function clearScore() {

  if (!state.isAdmin) { closeModal(); return; }

  if (!confirm("Clear this score and all match stats?")) return;

  delete state.scores[state.editingMatchId];

  saveState();

  closeModal();

  render();

}


// ============================================================

// MATCH RESULTS VIEW (read-only, everyone)

// ============================================================


function openResultsModal(matchId) {

  const match = DEFAULT_SCHEDULE.find(m => m.id === matchId);

  if (!match) return;

  const score = state.scores[matchId];

  const homeId = getMatchTeam(matchId, "home");

  const awayId = getMatchTeam(matchId, "away");


  document.getElementById("results-eyebrow").textContent = getMatchRoundLabel(match);

  document.getElementById("results-scoreline").innerHTML = `

    <span class="rs-team">${getTeamFlag(homeId)} ${getTeamDisplayName(homeId)}</span>

    <span class="rs-score">${score.home} <span class="dash">–</span> ${score.away}</span>

    <span class="rs-team">${getTeamDisplayName(awayId)} ${getTeamFlag(awayId)}</span>`;

  document.getElementById("results-sub").textContent =

    `${match.field} · Day ${match.day}, ${formatTime(match.time).time} ${formatTime(match.time).period}`;


  const ev = score.events || { goals: [], assists: [], saves: [] };

  const homeName = getTeamDisplayName(homeId), awayName = getTeamDisplayName(awayId);


  function statBlock(title, list) {

    if (!list || !list.length) return "";

    const side = t => t === "away" ? awayName : homeName;

    const items = list.map(e =>

      `<li><span class="re-player">${esc(e.player)}</span><span class="re-team">${esc(side(e.team))}</span></li>`

    ).join("");

    return `<div class="results-stat"><div class="results-stat-title">${title}</div><ul>${items}</ul></div>`;

  }


  const blocks = statBlock("Goals", ev.goals) + statBlock("Assists", ev.assists) + statBlock("Saves", ev.saves);

  document.getElementById("results-body").innerHTML = blocks ||

    `<div class="results-empty">No player stats recorded for this match.</div>`;


  // Admins get an "Edit result" shortcut.

  const editBtn = document.getElementById("results-edit");

  if (state.adminMode && homeId && awayId) {

    editBtn.style.display = "inline-flex";

    editBtn.onclick = () => { closeResultsModal(); openScoreModal(matchId); };

  } else {

    editBtn.style.display = "none";

  }


  document.getElementById("results-modal").classList.add("active");

}


function closeResultsModal() {

  document.getElementById("results-modal").classList.remove("active");

}


// ============================================================

// ADMIN LOGIN

// ============================================================


function openLoginModal() {

  const isIn = state.isAdmin;

  document.getElementById("login-error").textContent = "";

  document.getElementById("login-fields").style.display = isIn ? "none" : "block";

  document.getElementById("login-logout").style.display = isIn ? "inline-flex" : "none";

  document.getElementById("login-title").textContent = isIn ? "You're signed in" : "Staff Sign In";

  document.getElementById("login-sub").textContent = isIn

    ? `Signed in as ${state.adminEmail || "admin"}. You can record and clear scores.`

    : "Sign in with an approved Google account to record scores.";

  document.getElementById("login-modal").classList.add("active");

}


function closeLoginModal() {

  document.getElementById("login-modal").classList.remove("active");

}


function attemptLogin() {

  const errEl = document.getElementById("login-error");

  errEl.textContent = "";


  if (!window.FWC || !window.FWC.ready) {

    errEl.textContent = "Cloud sync isn't configured yet. Scores will stay on this device only.";

    return;

  }


  const btn = document.getElementById("login-google");

  btn.disabled = true;


  window.FWC.login()

    .then(result => {

      if (result && result.allowed) {

        // onAuthChange handles state + UI; just close.

        closeLoginModal();

      } else {

        const who = result && result.email ? result.email : "that account";

        errEl.textContent = `${who} isn't on the approved list. Ask the organizer to add it.`;

      }

    })

    .catch(err => {

      console.warn("Google sign-in failed:", err.code || err.message);

      // popup-closed-by-user is a normal cancel, not an error worth shouting about

      if (err.code !== "auth/popup-closed-by-user" && err.code !== "auth/cancelled-popup-request") {

        errEl.textContent = "Sign-in failed. Try again.";

      }

    })

    .finally(() => { btn.disabled = false; });

}


function attemptLogout() {

  if (window.FWC && window.FWC.ready) window.FWC.logout();

  closeLoginModal();

  // onAuthChange will flip state.isAdmin -> false and re-render.

}


// ============================================================

// EVENT LISTENERS

// ============================================================


document.getElementById("nav").addEventListener("click", e => {

  if (e.target.tagName !== "BUTTON") return;

  const page = e.target.dataset.page;

  document.querySelectorAll("#nav button").forEach(b => b.classList.toggle("active", b.dataset.page === page));

  document.querySelectorAll(".page").forEach(p => p.classList.toggle("active", p.id === `page-${page}`));

  window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });

});


document.getElementById("adminToggle").addEventListener("click", () => {

  // If not signed in as admin, clicking opens the login modal.

  if (!state.isAdmin) {

    openLoginModal();

    return;

  }

  // If already admin, the button toggles edit affordances on/off,

  // and a long-press / second purpose: offer logout via the modal.

  if (state.adminMode) {

    // Currently showing edit mode -> offer to log out.

    openLoginModal(); // modal detects admin state and shows logout

  } else {

    state.adminMode = true;

    refreshAdminButton();

    render();

  }

});


function refreshAdminButton() {

  const btn = document.getElementById("adminToggle");

  if (!state.isAdmin) {

    btn.textContent = "Admin · Log in";

    btn.classList.remove("on");

  } else {

    btn.textContent = state.adminMode ? "Admin · On" : "Admin · Off";

    btn.classList.toggle("on", state.adminMode);

  }

  // Draw tab is admin-only. If we just lost admin while on it, bounce to Overview.

  const drawNav = document.getElementById("nav-draw");

  if (drawNav) {

    drawNav.style.display = state.isAdmin ? "" : "none";

    if (!state.isAdmin) {

      const drawPage = document.getElementById("page-draw");

      if (drawPage && drawPage.classList.contains("active")) goToPage("overview");

    }

  }

}


// Programmatic page switch (mirrors the nav click handler).

function goToPage(page) {

  document.querySelectorAll("#nav button").forEach(b => b.classList.toggle("active", b.dataset.page === page));

  document.querySelectorAll(".page").forEach(p => p.classList.toggle("active", p.id === `page-${page}`));

}


document.getElementById("modal-save").addEventListener("click", saveScore);

document.getElementById("modal-cancel").addEventListener("click", closeModal);

document.getElementById("modal-clear").addEventListener("click", clearScore);

document.getElementById("modal").addEventListener("click", e => {

  if (e.target.id === "modal") closeModal();

});

document.getElementById("modal-home-score").addEventListener("input", updateStatsNote);

document.getElementById("modal-away-score").addEventListener("input", updateStatsNote);


document.getElementById("results-close").addEventListener("click", closeResultsModal);

document.getElementById("results-modal").addEventListener("click", e => {

  if (e.target.id === "results-modal") closeResultsModal();

});


document.getElementById("login-google").addEventListener("click", attemptLogin);

document.getElementById("login-cancel").addEventListener("click", closeLoginModal);

document.getElementById("login-logout").addEventListener("click", attemptLogout);

document.getElementById("login-modal").addEventListener("click", e => {

  if (e.target.id === "login-modal") closeLoginModal();

});


document.getElementById("draw-random").addEventListener("click", drawRandom);

document.getElementById("draw-reset").addEventListener("click", resetDraw);

document.getElementById("draw-modal-cancel").addEventListener("click", closeDrawModal);

document.getElementById("draw-modal-clear").addEventListener("click", clearDrawSlot);

document.getElementById("draw-modal").addEventListener("click", e => {

  if (e.target.id === "draw-modal") closeDrawModal();

});


document.getElementById("roster-modal-cancel").addEventListener("click", closeRosterModal);

document.getElementById("roster-modal-save").addEventListener("click", saveRosterEdits);

document.getElementById("roster-modal").addEventListener("click", e => {

  if (e.target.id === "roster-modal") closeRosterModal();

});


document.addEventListener("keydown", e => {

  if (e.key === "Escape" && document.getElementById("modal").classList.contains("active")) closeModal();

  if (e.key === "Escape" && document.getElementById("login-modal").classList.contains("active")) closeLoginModal();

  if (e.key === "Escape" && document.getElementById("draw-modal").classList.contains("active")) closeDrawModal();

  if (e.key === "Escape" && document.getElementById("roster-modal").classList.contains("active")) closeRosterModal();

  if (e.key === "Escape" && document.getElementById("results-modal").classList.contains("active")) closeResultsModal();

  if (e.key === "Enter" && document.getElementById("modal").classList.contains("active")) {

    if (document.activeElement.classList.contains("score-input")) saveScore();

  }

});


// ============================================================

// INIT

// ============================================================


// Kickoff: Tuesday, July 14, 2026 at 8:00 AM Eastern (EDT, UTC-4 in July).

// The fixed offset means every viewer counts down to the same moment,

// regardless of their device's timezone.

const KICKOFF = new Date("2026-07-14T08:00:00-04:00");


function updateCountdown() {

  const cd = document.getElementById("countdown");

  if (!cd) return;

  const diff = KICKOFF.getTime() - Date.now();


  if (diff <= 0) {

    // We've reached kickoff — stop counting, show zeros in green.

    cd.classList.add("started");

    setNum("cd-days", 0); setNum("cd-hours", 0); setNum("cd-mins", 0); setNum("cd-secs", 0);

    const tgt = cd.parentElement.querySelector(".cd-target");

    if (tgt) tgt.textContent = "Kicked off — Tuesday, July 14";

    return;

  }


  const s = Math.floor(diff / 1000);

  setNum("cd-days",  Math.floor(s / 86400));

  setNum("cd-hours", Math.floor((s % 86400) / 3600));

  setNum("cd-mins",  Math.floor((s % 3600) / 60));

  setNum("cd-secs",  s % 60);

}


function setNum(id, n) {

  const el = document.getElementById(id);

  if (el) el.textContent = (id === "cd-days") ? String(n) : String(n).padStart(2, "0");

}


loadState();      // local cache first, so something shows instantly / offline

refreshAdminButton();

render();

updateCountdown();

setInterval(updateCountdown, 1000);


setTimeout(() => {

  document.getElementById("loading").classList.add("hide");

}, 500);


// Connect to Firebase once the bridge module is available.

function connectFirebase() {

  if (!window.FWC || !window.FWC.ready) {

    setSyncStatus("offline");

    return;

  }


  setSyncStatus("connected");


  // Live updates: any change to the cloud doc updates every viewer.

  // We do NOT overwrite data that an admin is mid-edit on (score modal or

  // roster editor), to avoid yanking values out from under them.

  window.FWC.subscribe((data) => {

    state.assignments = data.assignments || {};

    if (state.editingMatchId === null) {

      state.scores = data.scores || {};

    }

    if (rosterEditingTeam === null) {

      state.rosters = data.rosters || {};

    }

    writeLocalCache();

    render();

  });


  // Track admin auth state. Payload: { isAdmin, email }.

  window.FWC.onAuthChange((info) => {

    state.isAdmin = info.isAdmin;

    state.adminEmail = info.email;

    if (!info.isAdmin) state.adminMode = false;

    else state.adminMode = true; // signing in turns on edit mode

    refreshAdminButton();

    render();

  });

}


// The module may finish before or after this script runs.

if (window.FWC) {

  connectFirebase();

} else {

  window.addEventListener("fwc-firebase-ready", connectFirebase, { once: true });

}


</script>
